qwen3-embedding:0.6b\n\n\ndef _ollama_embed(\n    texts: list[str],\n    *,\n    ollama_url: str = \"http://127.0.0.1:11434\",\n    model: str = \"qwen3-embedding:0.6b\",\n) -> list[list[float]]:\n    \"\"\"Get embeddings from Ollama API.\"\"\"\n    payload = json.dumps({\"model\": model, \"input\": texts}).encode()\n    req = urllib_request.Request(\n        f\"{ollama_url}/api/embed\",\n        data=payload,\n        headers={\"Content-Type\": \"application/json\"},\n    )\n    with urllib_request.urlopen(req, timeout=60) as resp:\n        data = json.load(resp)\n    return data[\"embeddings\"]\n\n\ndef _post_to_text(post: Post, clean_text: str = \"\") -> str:\n    \"\"\"Build a single string for embedding from post fields.\"\"\"\n    parts = [f\"r/{post.subreddit}\", post.title]\n    if clean_text:\n        parts.append(clean_text[:2000])\n    elif post.body:\n        parts.append(post.body[:2000])\n    if post.flair:\n        parts.append(f\"[{post.flair}]\")\n    return \"\\n\".join(parts)\n\n\n@dataclass(slots=True)\nclass QdrantStore:\n    url: str\n    api_key: str | None = None\n    posts_collection: str = \"reddit_posts_dense\"\n    ollama_url: str = \"http://127.0.0.1:11434\"\n    ollama_model: str = \"qwen3-embedding:0.6b\"\n    _client: QdrantClient = field(init=False, repr=False)\n\n    def __post_init__(self) -> None:\n        self._client = QdrantClient(\n            url=self.url,\n            api_key=self.api_key,\n            timeout=30,\n        )\n\n    # ── Bootstrap ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n    def ensure_collections(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Create collections if they don't exist.\"\"\"\n        existing = {c.name for c in self._client.get_collections().collections}\n        for name in (self.posts_collection,):\n            if name not in existing:\n                self._client.create_collection(\n                    collection_name=name,\n                    vectors_config=VectorParams(\n                        size=EMBEDDING_DIM,\n                        distance=Distance.COSINE,\n                    ),\n                )\n                logger.info(\"Created Qdrant collection: %s\", name)\n\n    # ── Upsert ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n    def upsert_post(self, post: Post, clean_text: str = \"\") -> None:\n        \"\"\"Embed and upsert a single post.\"\"\"\n        text = _post_to_text(post, clean_text)\n        embeddings = _ollama_embed(\n            [text], ollama_url=self.ollama_url, model=self.ollama_model\n        )\n        point_id = self._url_to_id(post.url)\n        payload = {\n            \"url\": post.url,\n            \"subreddit\": post.subreddit,\n            \"title\": post.title,\n            \"author\": post.author,\n            \"score\": post.score,\n            \"num_comments\": post.num_comments,\n            \"flair\": post.flair,\n            \"interest_score\": post.interest_score,\n            \"created_utc\": post.created_utc.isoformat(),\n            \"indexed_at\": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),\n        }\n        self._client.upsert(\n            collection_name=self.posts_collection,\n            points=[\n                PointStruct(id=point_id, vector=embeddings[0], payload=payload)\n            ],\n        )\n\n    def upsert_posts_batch(\n        self, posts: list[tuple[Post, str]], batch_size: int = 32\n    ) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Embed and upsert posts in batches. Each item is (post, clean_text).\"\"\"\n        total = 0\n        for i in range(0, len(posts), batch_size):\n            batch = posts[i : i + batch_size]\n            texts = [_post_to_text(p, ct) for p, ct in batch]\n            embeddings = _ollama_embed(\n                texts, ollama_url=self.ollama_url, model=self.ollama_model\n            )\n            points = []\n            for (post, _), vec in zip(batch, embeddings):\n                points.append(\n                    PointStruct(\n                        id=self._url_to_id(post.url),\n                        vector=vec,\n                        payload={\n                            \"url\": post.url,\n                            \"subreddit\": post.subreddit,\n                            \"title\": post.title,\n                            \"author\": post.author,\n                            \"score\": post.score,\n                            \"num_comments\": post.num_comments,\n                            \"flair\": post.flair,\n                            \"interest_score\": post.interest_score,\n                            \"created_utc\": post.created_utc.isoformat(),\n                            \"indexed_at\": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),\n                        },\n                    )\n                )\n            self._client.upsert(\n                collection_name=self.posts_collection, points=points\n            )\n            total += len(points)\n        return total\n\n    # ── Search ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n    def search_similar(\n        self,\n        query: str,\n        *,\n        subreddit: str | None = None,\n        limit: int = 10,\n        score_threshold: float = 0.3,\n    ) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"Semantic search for posts similar to query text.\"\"\"\n        embeddings = _ollama_embed(\n            [query], ollama_url=self.ollama_url, model=self.ollama_model\n        )\n        query_filter = None\n        if subreddit:\n            from qdrant_client.models import FieldCondition, Filter, MatchValue\n\n            query_filter = Filter(\n                must=[\n                    FieldCondition(\n                        key=\"subreddit\", match=MatchValue(value=subreddit)\n                    )\n                ]\n            )\n        results = self._client.query_points(\n            collection_name=self.posts_collection,\n            query=embeddings[0],\n            query_filter=query_filter,\n            limit=limit,\n            score_threshold=score_threshold,\n        )\n        return [\n            {**point.payload, \"_score\": point.score}\n            for point in results.points\n        ]\n\n    def count_posts(self) -> int:\n        info = self._client.get_collection(self.posts_collection)\n        return info.points_count\n\n    # {"type":"item.completed","item":{"id":"item_56","type":"agent_message","text":"**Plan**\n- `hybrid-store` is coupled to ES and Qdrant in three places, not one: [hybrid_store/store.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/hybrid-store/hybrid_store/store.py#L24), [hybrid_store/hybrid_search.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/hybrid-store/hybrid_store/hybrid_search.py#L96), and [hybrid_store/reader.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/hybrid-store/hybrid_store/reader.py#L117). The migration should introduce `hybrid_store/pg_store.py` as the single PostgreSQL backend, then keep `HybridStore` as a compatibility facade over it.\n- I’d use `psycopg` + `psycopg_pool.ConnectionPool`, not `asyncpg`, because the current callers are synchronous. Make `DATABASE_URL` the canonical env var, keep `OLLAMA_*`, add pool knobs like `PG_POOL_MIN_SIZE` and `PG_POOL_MAX_SIZE`, and set `prepare_threshold=None` so Neon pooled connections do not trip over server-side prepares.\n- Preserve the current `HybridStore` surface for `swimswam`: `write_title`, `read_title`, `list_pending`, `list_processing`, `update_fetch_status`, `upsert_article`, `upsert_article_chunks`, `search`, `get_count`, `normalize_url`, and `url_id` from [hybrid_store/store.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/hybrid-store/hybrid_store/store.py#L155). `ensure_collections()` should become a schema-validation alias, not a real DDL step.\n- Rewrite search in SQL. For FTS, use `websearch_to_tsquery('english', $1)` against `fts` with `ts_rank_cd`. For vector search, order by `embedding <=> $query::halfvec(1024)`. For hybrid, run FTS and vector candidate CTEs and fuse them with RRF, keeping the return shape from [hybrid_store/hybrid_search.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/hybrid-store/hybrid_store/hybrid_search.py#L257).\n- Replace the ES-specific reader logic in [hybrid_store/reader.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/hybrid-store/hybrid_store/reader.py#L262) with PostgreSQL keyset pagination over `(sort_field, url)`. That is the direct replacement for ES `search_after`.\n\n**Caller Rollout**\n- `swimswam` should need minimal code churn because it only talks to `HybridStore` in [sync_titles.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/swimswam/sync_titles.py#L29) and [fetch_articles.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/swimswam/fetch_articles.py#L226). Most of the work is inside `hybrid-store`, plus swapping `.env` from ES/Qdrant settings to `DATABASE_URL`.\n- `grow-in-reddit` needs a real storage refactor. It currently has two separate adapters in [storage/es_store.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/grow-in-reddit/storage/es_store.py#L68) and [storage/qdrant_store.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/grow-in-reddit/storage/qdrant_store.py#L54), wired through [collector/article_store.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/grow-in-reddit/collector/article_store.py#L33) and [main.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/grow-in-reddit/main.py#L80). Replace those with one `storage/postgres_store.py`, then collapse the builder/config logic in [settings.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/grow-in-reddit/settings.py#L20) and [main.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/grow-in-reddit/main.py#L116).\n- Standardize embeddings on Ollama `/api/embed` batching. `grow-in-reddit` already does that in [storage/qdrant_store.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/grow-in-reddit/storage/qdrant_store.py#L24); `hybrid-store` still uses the older `/api/embeddings` shape in [hybrid_store/embedder.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/hybrid-store/hybrid_store/embedder.py#L17).\n\n**Assumptions And Risks**\n- The provided schema stores one `embedding` per article/post. That is a real behavior change from the current chunk-level dense indexing in [hybrid_store/store.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/hybrid-store/hybrid_store/store.py#L284). If chunk-level recall still matters, a chunk table should be added later; otherwise the migration should explicitly accept article-level semantic search.\n- PostgreSQL FTS is not exact BM25. With the installed extensions and schema, the practical implementation is `ts_rank_cd` over `tsvector`. If exact BM25 is a hard requirement, that needs a different scoring path.\n- `from hybrid_store import HybridStore` is already broken today: `python3 -c \"from hybrid_store import HybridStore\"` fails with `ModuleNotFoundError: elasticsearch` because [hybrid_store/__init__.py](/home/ubuntu/scripts/hybrid-store/hybrid_store/__init__.py#L1) eagerly imports ES-backed modules. The PostgreSQL cutover should remove that dependency chain entirely.\n\nIf you want the implementation pass next, the clean order is `config.py` -> `pg_store.py` -> `store.py` facade -> `hybrid_search.py`/`reader.py` -> `swimswam` -> `grow-in-reddit`."}}
